<review>Very enjoyable mountain course,  but too unplayable for some.  Played with a fun couple last week, and they liked it but will not be back.

Depending on pin placement you may have the most three putts in your life.

In general, you need to hit it long, straight, and have a good short game.  No forgiveness being off the fairway, as the ball will be unplayable IF you can find it.

Even a good drive can leave a bad lie given the hilly nature of most holes.</review>< pictures>

< review>
Love this park! Hands down ome of my kids favorite parks. They love they play structure that resembles a rocket/space ship. They have swings for big kids and babies, they have a splash pad and an ample amount of running room. Tons of picnic areas, so a great place to have a party, they have the splash pad which is a huge plus especially in the summer. They also have a section for dogs, which is also fun for the kids. Though i do not let my kids in with the dogs (some people do that there, so dog folks be ware) I do let them watch the dogs from outside the fence. No joke my kids could sit for hours and watch the dogs play. Anyways, lots of fun, lots to do, and lots of space.</review>

< text>
My girlfriend and I brought our dogs here for a little doggies day and I was so impressed. There were two separate sections, one for small dogs and one for big dogs. We took our dogs, Lucy and Winnie, into the big dog section. It was a Tuesday but the park was packed full of doggies. <Rate>2</Rate>< Review>
This dog park is a decent size and the gates and fence are secure. The problem lies with all dog parks, people don't look after their dogs and there are frequent fights. The rest of the park is nice, there is a great playground for children as well as a water park for little ones to cool off in the summer. If you are used to the problems of other people not being able to manage their own dogs, then this dog park might be worth a visit, but if you are looking for an outing with your pup amonst responsible pet owners with well trained animals you might want to give this place a miss.<//Review>

< review>
Lots of parking, restrooms are close by, and there's lights on til 10-1030 pm. Like with any park, survey the dogs inside before entering, the large side can get rough because of irresponsible owners not keeping their dogs in check. As for the people park, watch out for bones and food in the grass as you walk to the dog park, weekend partiers are huge litterers. And there has been an increase in homeless presence, but they mostly keep to themselves.</review>
